<script type="text/javascript">
var activeAbs = {"62":{"c":"5","d":"95"},"77":{"d":"75","e":"10","f":"10","c":"5"}};

function runAb(name) {
    if ( !activeAbs || !activeAbs[name] ) {
        return null;
    }
    try {
        var cookie_val = PH.cookie.get("aboption");
        if (cookie_val) {
            cookie_val = decodeURIComponent(cookie_val);
        }
        var abOpt = JSON.parse(cookie_val);
    } catch (e) {}

    if ( abOpt &amp;&amp; abOpt[name] &amp;&amp; activeAbs[name][abOpt[name]] ) {
        return abOpt[name];
    }
    var currentOpt = generateAb(activeAbs[name]);
    if ( currentOpt ) {
        recordAB(abOpt, name, currentOpt);
    }
    return currentOpt;
}

function recordAB(abOpt, name, currentOpt) {
    if ( !abOpt ) {
        abOpt = {};
    } else {
        for (opt in abOpt) {
            if ( !activeAbs[opt] ) {
                delete abOpt[opt];
            }
        };
    }

    abOpt[name] = currentOpt;
    PH.cookie.set(
            'aboption',
            encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify(abOpt)),
            30,
            '/',
            '.emag.ro'
    );

    reqwest({
        url: EM.old_site_endpoint + "/ablogger.php?name=" + name + "&amp;value=" + currentOpt + "&amp;source=www",
        data: {},
        method: 'GET',
        type: 'json',
        crossOrigin: true
    });
}

function generateAb(distribution) {
    var limit = 0;
    var rnd = Math.floor(Math.random() * 100 + 1);
    var curOpt = lastOpt = null;

    for (index in distribution) {
        lastOpt = index;
        limit += parseFloat(distribution[index]);
        if ( rnd &lt;= limit ) {
            curOpt = index;
            break;
        }
    }

    if ( curOpt ) {
        return curOpt;
    } else {
        return lastOpt;
    }
}

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(event) {
    //run ab here, ex: runAb(12);
});
</script>

    </div>
